The relevance of psychiatry to top-level performance is increasingly apparent,
and nowhere more so than in the world of athletics. For years athletes have
tried to gain a competitive edge by finding ways to directly enhance their
performance. In the new era of sports, with its increased pressures of public
scrutiny and demands, it is equally important to eliminate distractions.
Psychiatrists and therapists who work with athletes play key roles in helping
athletes calm the emotional and social storm that could potentially hinder
athletic success.  
  
  
The NCAA states that out of every 10,000 high school senior boys playing
basketball only 3 will make it to the NBA (0.03%). This statistic reveals the
enormous talent of those who make it to the top; they are extraordinarily
gifted,[jordan 4 cavs for sale](http://www.jordanspacejams2u.com/cheap-

are the valued connections that make it possible for star athletes to
survive,[url](http://www.redsoleclshoes.com/ "http://www.redsoleclshoes.com/"
), thrive, and achieve lasting success.

"http://shop.jordansshoestore.com/" ). The athlete's talent can take them
places that their character may not be prepared to keep them. The signing of a
multimillion dollar contract does not make one an instant professional,
especially if the athlete is a teenager who just finished high school.  
  
  
Therefore, it is often the quality of healthy connections that provide a
crucial sense of security in the chaotic world of sports. Because there are so
many people focusing attention, making requests, and asking for time, trust
becomes a central issue. People make decisions based on the advice of those
they trust.  
  
  
Sometimes, however, the person the athlete trusts is not actually qualified to
make appropriate decisions. There is a high level of trust, for instance, in
the friend who had your back on the playground or who protected you from
gangs, but is this the person who should be advising you on business matters?  
  
The spotlight of success brings with it a barrage of complex
decisions,[redsoleclshoes.com](http://www.redsoleclshoes.com/
"http://www.redsoleclshoes.com/" ), as well as constant demands from family,

key to healthy athletic success is appropriately and profitably managing the
social and psychological impact of their performance.

Below are profiles of two admired Lakers players, Derek Fisher and Pau Gasol.

Derek Fisher  
  
Derek Lamar Fisher is the younger brother of former NBA player, Duane
Washington. Fisher plays point guard for the LA Lakers at jersey number 2.
Fisher was born on August
9,[nike.jordansshoestore.com](http://nike.jordansshoestore.com/
"http://nike.jordansshoestore.com/" ), 1974 in Little Rock, Arkansas. He has
four children to wife,<http://www.realauthenticjordans.com/>, Candace.  
  
Fisher went to high school in Parkview Arts and Sciences Magnet and was a
basketball letterman. After high school, Fisher proceeded to the University of
Arkansas at Little Rock (UALR) where he majored in communications and
established a school record for free throws 399. In UALR, Fisher also took
third place among all-time UALR leaders in three-point field goals made (125)
and earned a Sunbelt Conference Player of the Year.  
  
Fisher played for three teams during his career, the LA Lakers first, the
Golden State Warriors next, and the Utah Jazz third, before returning to the
Lakers. During his first stint with the Lakers, Fisher made headlines by
making a successful final shot in the team's 5th game against the Spurs within
0.4 seconds. He then joined the Warriors after being offered $37 million over
six years. Disappointed that he was unable to run his own game with the
Warriors, Fisher was traded to the Jazz for Andre Owens, Devin Brown, and
Keith McLeod.  
  
It was during his stint with the Jazz that Fisher once again made headlines.
He was unavailable for the opening of the 2007 NBA Playoffs,[jordan 6 retro
for sale](http://www.ajordan12playoffs.com/air-jordan-6-retro-c-51.html
"http://www.ajordan12playoffs.com/air-jordan-6-retro-c-51.html" ), Jazz
against Spurs, because of his daughter's physical condition. But right at the
time his team needed him most, Fisher appeared at the court straight from his
daughter's eye surgery and helped the Jazz win Game 2.  
  
Now that Fisher is with the Lakers for the second time, he, along with Kobe
Bryant, provides veteran influence to younger members. The Lakers played
against Jazz in the 2008 NBA
Playoffs,[shop.jordansshoestore](http://shop.jordansshoestore.com/

) Fisher played a bigger role for his team.  
  
Paul Gasol  
  
Pau Gasol Saez was born on July 6, 1980 in Barcelona, Catalonia, Spain. He is
the son of Agusti and Marisa Gasol, with two younger brothers, Adria and Marc,
also an NBA player. Gasol is the power forward and center of the LA Lakers. He
holds jersey number 16 and will soon mark hist first year with the LA Lakers.  
  
Gasol started playing basketball for his school team in Spain. At 16, Gasol
played for Barcelona's junior team that won the 1998 FIBA Europe Under-18
Championship and the 1998 Albert Schweitzer Tournament. Gasol also played and
continues to do so for Spain in various basketball events including the
European and World Championships as well as the Olympics.  
  
Gasol was drafted into the NBA in 2001 by the Atlanta Hawks but was traded to

##  authentic jordans for sale Dallas Mavericks Tickets The Mid-

The Dallas Mavericks are a professional basketball team based in Dallas,
Texas, USA. They are members of the Southwest Division of the Western
Conference of the National Basketball Association (NBA). Founded in 1980, the
Mavericks have won three division titles and one conference championship
(2006).  
  
According to a 2011 Forbes Magazine report, they are the sixth most valuable
basketball franchise in the United States, valued at approximately $438
million; the franchise is surpassed in value only by the New York Knicks, the
Los Angeles
Lakers,[nike.jordansshoestore.com](http://nike.jordansshoestore.com/
"http://nike.jordansshoestore.com/" ), the Chicago Bulls, the Boston Celtics,
and the Houston Rockets.  
  
For much of the 1980s, the Mavericks boast a very good team in the highly
competitive Western Conference. Led by Mark Aguirre, original draft pick Brad
Davis, Rolando Blackman, Derek
Harper,[uptempoair](http://www.nicekicks.webebden.net/air-jordan-4-fusion-
whitevarsity-redblack-p-173.htmll "http://www.nicekicks.webebden.net/air-
jordan-4-fusion-whitevarsity-redblack-p-173.htmll" ), Sam Perkins and Detlef
Schrempf,[buy real jordan](http://www.wheretobuyauthenticjordans.com/
"http://www.wheretobuyauthenticjordans.com/" ), the Mavericks made the
playoffs six of seven times from 1983/90, winning the Midwest Division in
1986-87 and reaching the Western Conference Finals in 1988. However, they
never made it deeper in the playoffs, due to the dominance of the Los Angeles
Lakers at the time.  
  
The 1990s were known as the Mavs' "dark ages". They never reached the playoffs
from 1991 through 2000, bottoming out with an 11-71 record in 1992-93 and a
13-69 mark in 1993-94. Much of their freefall was blamed for various off-court
and on-court distractions, particularly Roy Tarpley's drug abuse,[jordan 3
cement](http://www.authenticrealjordans.com/AuthenticJordans-Cheap-3-42
"http://www.authenticrealjordans.com/AuthenticJordans-Cheap-3-42" ), which
eventually got him banned from the NBA, and the injuries and former coach
Quinn Buckner's disciplinary approach.  
  
The mid-90s were considered the only positive period for the Mavs, led by The
3 J's: Jason Kidd, Jim Jackson and Jamal Mashburn. Kidd would become the most
famous of the trio, winning Co-Rookie of the Year (with Grant Hill) in 1994-95
and eventually a perennial All-Star.  
  
The Mavericks returned to prominence in the 2000s, first led by a new "Big
Three" of Dirk Nowitzki, Michael Finley and Steve Nash. With a new owner in
Mark Cuban and head coach Don Nelson leading the crew,[cheap jordan 5
shoes](http://www.realjordanssale.com/air-jordan-mens-shoes-nike-air-jordan-
retro-5-c-9_14.html "http://www.realjordanssale.com/air-jordan-mens-shoes-
nike-air-jordan-retro-5-c-9_14.html" ), they returned to the playoffs in 2001,
eventually returning to the Conference Finals in 2003. However the San Antonio
Spurs would emerge as their main rivals, defeating them in the playoffs each
time.  
  
Nowitzki emerged as the team's leader, and with Avery Johnson coaching the
team, the Mavericks would make their first NBA Finals appearance in 2006;
along the way exacting revenge against the Spurs and defeating Steve Nash and
the Suns. However after leading 2-0 to the Miami Heat, they lost the Finals'
next four games, though some point to biased referring and others argue it was
the result of the Curse of the Crease.  
  
The Mavs' best regular season came in 2006-07, winning 67 games and earned the
NBA's best record. Despite Nowitzki's MVP showing, the Mavericks were upset by
their former coach Don Nelson and the 8th seeded Golden State Warriors in the
2007 NBA Playoffs. Kidd returned to the team in 2008, and with new coach Rick
Carlisle leading the crew, the Mavericks maintained their winning form
throughout the decade.

##  jordan 12 playoffs Understanding NBA betting odds

If you love watching NBA games, you will surely love betting on it too! NBA
betting double the excitement and fun as we watch our favorite NBA sport.
However, betting on a popular sport like NBA comes a little tough most
especially if you don have concrete ideas to base your betting choices. This
derived the NBA betting odds. So,[retro jordans](http://www.kickzd.com/
"http://www.kickzd.com/" ), what is it all about?  
  
NBA betting odds is actually a system
w[here](http://shop.jordansshoestore.com/ "http://shop.jordansshoestore.com/"
) all the basic sources to base all your betting choices in every basketball
game can be found. It is a system that helps you bet particular amounts while
illustrating all the possible prospects of your preferred team winning the
game. The data that are given in the system came from a long list of
sportsbook and totaled from every basketball match.  
  
  
The NBA betting odds is categorized into significant segments composed of the
date and time of competition, rotation
number,[nike.jordansshoestore.com](http://nike.jordansshoestore.com/
"http://nike.jordansshoestore.com/" ), teams playing against each other, point
spread, money line and total. It is necessary that you are aware of these
terms to be successful in your NBA bet.  
  
 ?The game roster is noted on the date and time while the rotation number
lists down the name of the visiting team over the home team.  
  
 ?The point spread, which is the most common bet not just in basketball but to
all sports, points out the favorite team from the underdog. For example, a
game between the Boston Celtics and LA Lakers comes up with a +7 as well as
-7, which means,[www.realjordanssale.com](http://www.realjordanssale.com/
"http://www.realjordanssale.com/" ), you are able to gain cash if Boston wins
the game right away or loses to LA with less than 7 points in the game.  
  
 ?The moneyline is simply betting on which team you think will win. The basis
of the betting volume is $ 100. For instance, the money line presents Dallas
Mavericks with a -340 and Boston Celtics with +320. This indicates that you
must bet $ 340 on Dallas to win $ 100, as well as a $ 100 bet on Boston to
obtain $ 320.  
  
The total, which is the easiest type of NBA bet, means betting on the sum of
all points from both teams. The ypothesized?figure is based on a substantial
guess obtained from sports analysis. If the total is 170 and the actual points
amount to 180,[afreshkicks.com](http://www.afreshkicks.com/
"http://www.afreshkicks.com/" ), then those who bet above 170 gains the cash.  
  
Understanding and learning how to read the NBA betting odds is very essential
to get a bigger chance of winning your hard earned money. Also, it can provide
you better understanding on exactly how the game affects the bets you are
willing to wager upon. So, be sure that you have study NBA betting odds prior
betting. Good Luck,[美国原装伟哥](http://20121545.blog.hexun.com/
"http://20121545.blog.hexun.com/" )!
